<DIV class="dclr"></DIV>
<P class="p0 ft0">Regeringens proposition 2024/25:106</P>
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t0">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr0 td0"><SPAN class="p1 ft1">Sveriges tillträde till konventionen om</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr0 td1"><SPAN class="p2 ft1">Prop.</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr1 td0"><SPAN class="p1 ft1">upprättande av Square Kilometre Array</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr1 td1"><SPAN class="p2 ft1">2024/25:106</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr2 td2"><SPAN class="p1 ft1">Observatory</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr2 td3"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p4 ft3">Regeringen överlämnar denna proposition till riksdagen.</P>
<P class="p5 ft3">Stockholm den 13 februari 2025</P>
<P class="p6 ft4">Ulf Kristersson</P>
<P class="p7 ft4">Johan Pehrson <SPAN class="ft3">(Utbildningsdepartementet)</SPAN></P>
<P class="p8 ft1">Propositionens huvudsakliga innehåll</P>
<P class="p9 ft3">Regeringen beslutade den 17 oktober 2024 – med förbehåll för ratificering</P>
<P class="p10 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">–</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">att konventionen av den 12 mars 2019 om upprättande av Square Kilometre Array Observatory ska undertecknas, vilket skedde den 21 januari 2025. I denna proposition föreslås att riksdagen ska godkänna Sveriges tillträde till konventionen. Enligt konventionen ska organisationen och vissa fysiska personer beviljas viss immunitet och vissa privilegier. Det föreslås därför att riksdagen beslutar om en ändring i lagen (1976:661) om immunitet och privilegier i vissa fall. Lagändringen föreslås träda i kraft den dag som regeringen bestämmer.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p11 ft3">1</P>
</DIV>

<P class="p5 ft3">Regeringens förslag:</P>
<P class="p20 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft8">Riksdagen godkänner Sveriges tillträde till konventionen om upprättande av Square Kilometre Array Observatory (avsnitt 6).</SPAN></P>
<P class="p21 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft8">Riksdagen antar regeringens förslag till lag om ändring i lagen (1976:661) om immunitet och privilegier i vissa fall.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p22 ft3">3</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_4">
<DIV id="p4dimg1">
<INGENBILD zsrc="HC031064x1.jpg/" id="p4img1">
</DIV>


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t3">

	<TD class="tr12 td15"><SPAN class="p3 ft1">Förslag till lag om ändring i lagen</SPAN> </TD>

	<TD class="tr5 td14"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>

	<TD class="tr1 td15"><SPAN class="p3 ft1">i vissa fall</SPAN> </TD>

<P class="p23 ft3">Härigenom föreskrivs att bilagan till lagen (1976:661) om immunitet och privilegier i vissa fall<A href="#page_4"><SPAN class="ft10">1 </SPAN></A>ska ha följande lydelse.</P>
<P class="p24 ft3">Denna lag träder i kraft den dag som regeringen bestämmer.</P>

</TR>
<TR>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr5 td56"><SPAN class="p44 ft3">Square Kilometre Array (SKA) är ett radioteleskop under uppbyggnad</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr7 td56"><SPAN class="p44 ft3">genom ett globalt samarbete under överinseende av den internationella</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr6 td56"><SPAN class="p44 ft3">organisationen Square Kilometre Array Observatory (SKAO). Konven-</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr7 td56"><SPAN class="p44 ft3">tionen av den 12 mars 2019 om upprättande av Square Kilometre Array</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr6 td56"><SPAN class="p44 ft3">Observatory trädde i kraft den 15 januari 2021. Enligt artikel 19 i konven-</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr6 td56"><SPAN class="p44 ft19">tionen ska den vara öppen för undertecknande och föremål för ratificering,</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr6 td56"><SPAN class="p44 ft3">godtagande, godkännande eller anslutning. Konventionen har ratificerats</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr7 td56"><SPAN class="p44 ft3">av Australien, Indien, Italien, Kina, Nederländerna, Portugal, Spanien,</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr6 td56"><SPAN class="p44 ft3">Storbritannien och Sydafrika. Vetenskapsrådet har begärt att Sverige ska</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr7 td56"><SPAN class="p44 ft3">tillträda konventionen (dnr U2022/00702). Begäran stöds av Verket för</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>

	<TD colspan=2 class="tr6 td56"><SPAN class="p44 ft3">innovationssystem (Vinnova) och Chalmers Tekniska Högskola</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>

</TR>
<TR>

</TR>
<TR>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr7 td56"><SPAN class="p44 ft3">ring – att konventionen ska undertecknas, vilket skedde den 21 januari</SPAN> </TD>

<TR>

	<TD class="tr0 td58"><SPAN class="p46 ft1">Vad är Square Kilometre Array</SPAN> </TD>

<TR>
	<TD class="tr5 td57"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td43"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td58"><SPAN class="p46 ft1">Observatory?</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr19 td57"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr19 td59"><SPAN class="p45 ft3">Square Kilometre Array Observatory (SKAO) är en internationell organi-</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr6 td57"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr6 td59"><SPAN class="p45 ft3">sation som leder ett globalt projekt med målet att bygga världens mest</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr6 td57"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr6 td59"><SPAN class="p45 ft3">kraftfulla radioteleskop, Square Kilometre Array (SKA). SKA är inte ett</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr7 td57"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr7 td59"><SPAN class="p45 ft3">enskilt teleskop utan en samling av teleskop, eller antenner, som placeras</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr6 td57"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr6 td59"><SPAN class="p45 ft3">ut i Australien och Sydafrika. SKAO:s globala högkvarter ligger vid</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>

<P class="p47 ft3">på olika sätt bidrar till projektet eller deltar som observatörer, däribland Prop. 2024/25:106 Frankrike, Japan, Kanada, Tyskland, Schweiz och Sydkorea. Sverige har</P>
<P class="p48 ft3">med sina deltagande forskare varit bland de drivande länderna i den vetenskapliga, tekniska och organisatoriska utvecklingen sedan 2011.</P>
<P class="p49 ft20">5 Vad innebär konventionen om upprättande av Square Kilometre Array Observatory?</P>
<P class="p50 ft21">Konventionens huvudsakliga innehåll</P>
<P class="p51 ft3">Konventionen om upprättande av Square Kilometre Array Observatory omfattar en inledning och 20 artiklar. Till konventionen har fogats två bilagor, ett protokoll om privilegier och immunitet och ett finansprotokoll. Bägge protokollen är integrerade delar av konventionen. I det följande anges det huvudsakliga innehållet i konventionen och de två bilagorna.</P>
<P class="p52 ft14">Ingressen</P>
<P class="p53 ft3">I ingressen bekräftar parterna att de vill genomföra ett av <NOBR>2000-talets</NOBR> mest visionära och ambitiösa forskningsprojekt som inbegriper ett betydelsefullt internationellt samarbete. Dessutom bekräftar parterna att de är fast beslutna att testa gränserna för de tekniska och vetenskapliga ansträngningarna och utforska grundläggande frågor inom astronomi och fysik. Parterna konstaterar också att Square Kilometre Array kommer att vara nästa generations radioteleskopanläggning med långt större upptäcktspotential än något tidigare instrument.</P>
<P class="p54 ft14">Artikel 1</P>
<P class="p55 ft3">I konventionens artikel 1 finns definitioner där det anges att med ”SKAO” avses Square Kilometre Array Observatory och andra definitioner av betydelse för förståelsen av konventionen. Exempelvis definieras ”personal” som anställda eller utstationerade personer vid SKAO och med uttrycket ”officiell verksamhet” avses enligt definitionen all verksamhet som bedrivs i enlighet med konventionen, inbegripet SKAO:s administrativa verksamhet.</P>

<DIV id="page_9">


<P class="p47 ft3">agera och rösta för medlemmens räkning. Rådet ska ansvara för den Prop. 2024/25:106 övergripande strategiska och vetenskapliga ledningen av SKAO, utse generaldirektören och godkänna utnämningen av andra högre tjänstemän</P>
<P class="p58 ft3">samt godkänna budgeten och övervaka utgifter och finansiell verksamhet. Varje medlem ska som huvudregel ha en röst i rådet. Rådet ska välja en ordförande och en vice ordförande för en mandatperiod på två år. Ordföranden och vice ordföranden får inte väljas mer än två gånger. Rådet ska upprätta en finanskommitté som varje medlem ska vara representerad i. Rådet ska också upprätta sådana andra kommittéer som kan behövas för att fullgöra SKAO:s syfte.</P>
<P class="p52 ft14">Artikel 9</P>
<P class="p59 ft3">Generaldirektören ska utses av rådet och då för en tidsbegränsad period. Rådet får när som helst avsluta generaldirektörens uppdrag i enlighet med den arbetsordning som ska godkännas av rådet. Generaldirektören ska vara verkställande direktör för SKAO och vara dess juridiska ombud. Generaldirektören ska rapportera till rådet. I generaldirektörens uppgifter ingår att ansvara för ledningen av SKAO, lämna budgetberäkningar, årsredovisning och det reviderade årsbokslutet till rådet. Generaldirektören ska bistås av den vetenskapliga, tekniska och administrativa personal som generaldirektören anser nödvändig inom de gränser som rådet har godkänt. Den personalen ska tillsättas och avsättas av generaldirektören i enlighet med tjänsteföreskrifterna.</P>
<P class="p60 ft14">Artikel 10 och finansprotokollet</P>
<P class="p55 ft3">Medlemmar och associerade medlemmar ska ha andelar i <NOBR>SKA-projektet</NOBR> som står i proportion till de sammanlagda finansiella bidrag som de åtagit sig att lämna till <NOBR>SKA-projektet</NOBR> (artikel 10.4). När det gäller finansiella frågor i övrigt hänvisas i konventionens artikel 10 till en bilaga till konventionen, bilaga B, som utgör finansprotokollet. Finansprotokollet som är en integrerad del av konventionen, innehåller i huvudsak följande.</P>
<P class="p61 ft3">SKAO ska följa principerna om sund ekonomisk förvaltning, effektivitet, öppenhet och ansvarighet vid planeringen och förvaltningen av finansiella resurser. Det ska finnas en finansieringsplan som enhälligt ska godkännas av rådet. Varje medlem och associerad medlem ska bidra i enlighet med gällande finansieringsplan. En inledande finansieringsplan ska enhälligt godkännas vid det första mötet i rådet eller så snart som det är lämpligt därefter. Rådet får göra översyner av finansieringsplanerna i syfte att vid behov ändra dessa i enlighet med de finansiella reglerna och rådet får när som helst enhälligt besluta att ändra en finansieringsplan men måste göra detta innan den berörda finansieringsplanen har löpt ut. Rådet får också enhälligt besluta att lägga till nya medlemmar och associerade medlemmar i en finansieringsplan, enligt de villkor som rådet föreskriver. Ingen översyn eller ändring av en finansieringsplan får dock resultera i en ändring av de finansiella bidrag som en medlem eller associerad medlem ska lämna, utan den medlemmens eller associerade medlemmens samtycke. Vidare gäller att rådet ska godkänna budgetar med dubbel majoritet. Med dubbel majoritet avses att ett och samma beslut godkänns med både</P>
<P class="p62 ft3">två tredjedels majoritet utifrån en viktad omröstning och två tredjedels</P>
<P class="p63 ft3">9</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_10">
<DIV id="p10dimg1">
<INGENBILD zsrc="HC0310610x1.jpg/" id="p10img1">
</DIV>


<P class="p64 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106 majoritet utifrån antalet närvarande och röstande medlemmar. Med viktad omröstning avses varje medlems användning av rösträtter i beslutsfattandet. En rösträtt fastställs utifrån varje medlems aktuella andel av projektet, i enlighet med finansieringsplanen. SKAO får, efter rådets godkännande, ta lån och ådra sig skulder, inom de gränser som anges i de finansiella reglerna. Ingen medlem eller associerad medlem ska ådra sig några ytterligare finansiella skyldigheter gentemot SKAO till följd av ett beslut att ta ett lån eller ådra sig skuld utan att uttryckligen ha samtyckt till att ådra sig en sådan skyldighet.</P>
<P class="p65 ft14">Artiklarna <NOBR>11–13</NOBR></P>
<P class="p66 ft3">SKAO ska ha en immaterialrättspolicy som enhälligt godkänns av rådet och rådet får besluta att bevilja tillgång till immateriella förgrundsrättigheter på visst sätt (artikel 11). Organisationen ska också ha en upphandlingspolicy och en verksamhetspolicy som enhälligt ska godkännas av rådet. Tillgången till tid med SKA fastställs i enlighet med en tillgångspolicy som enhälligt godkänns av rådet. Alla rådets ändringar av tillgångspolicyn ska kräva två tredjedels majoritet, utom de bestämmelser som enligt policyn ska kräva enhällighet för att ändras. SKAO ska bedriva sin verksamhet enligt principen att medlemmars och associerade medlemmars tillgång står i proportion till deras andel av projektet, om inte rådet enhälligt har beslutat annat (artiklarna 12 och 13).</P>
<P class="p67 ft14">Artiklarna <NOBR>14–20</NOBR></P>
<P class="p66 ft3">Konventionen innehåller också allmänna bestämmelser om tvistlösning, ändringar av konventionen, frånträde, uppsägning, upplösning och bestämmelser om vad som händer om en medlem underlåter att fullgöra sina skyldigheter som åligger medlemmen enligt konventionen (artiklarna 14 – 18).</P>
<P class="p68 ft3">Slutligen anges att konventionen ska vara föremål för ratificering, godtagande eller godkännande av de stater som anges i konventionen (bland andra Sverige) i enlighet med deras inhemska krav. Regeringen för Förenade konungariket Storbritannien och Nordirland ska vara depositarie för konventionen. För stater eller internationella organisationer som deponerar sitt <NOBR>ratifikations-,</NOBR> <NOBR>godtagande-,</NOBR> godkännande- eller anslutningsinstrument efter det att konventionen har trätt i kraft ska konventionen träda i kraft trettio dagar efter den dag då dess <NOBR>ratifikations-,</NOBR> <NOBR>godtagande-,</NOBR> godkännande- eller anslutningsinstrument deponerades (artiklarna <NOBR>19–20).</NOBR></P>
<P class="p69 ft1"><SPAN class="ft1">6</SPAN><SPAN class="ft23">Godkännande av Sveriges tillträde till konventionen</SPAN></P>
<P class="p70 ft3"><SPAN class="ft14">Regeringens förslag: </SPAN>Riksdagen godkänner att Sverige tillträder konventionen om upprättande av Square Kilometre Array Observatory.</P>
<P class="p71 ft3">10</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_11">


<P class="p72 ft3"><SPAN class="ft14">Skälen för regeringens förslag: </SPAN>Square Kilometre Array kommer Prop. 2024/25:106 enligt planerna bli världens i särklass mest kraftfulla radioteleskop och är</P>
<P class="p73 ft3">ett av världens högst rankade vetenskapliga projekt. Vetenskapsrådet anger i sin begäran om att Sverige ska tillträda konventionen att Vetenskapsrådet bedömer att det vetenskapliga värdet av deltagande i SKAO är högt och att Verket för innovationssystem stöder Vetenskapsrådets begäran. Chalmers Tekniska Högskola Aktiebolag har i skrivelse till regeringen angett att de anser att medlemskapet innebär stora möjligheter till såväl teknikutveckling som affärsmöjligheter för svenska företag inom för Sverige strategiskt viktiga områden. Observatoriet öppnar upp för ny vetenskap och syftar till att besvara en mängd fundamentala frågor relaterade till bland annat uppkomst av liv samt universums uppbyggnad och utveckling. SKAO har också betydelse för utveckling av teknik och metoder för hantering och analys av de enorma datamängder som kommer att genereras. Utvecklingen sker i samarbete med European Organization for Nuclear Research (CERN) och medlemsländerna och väntas bana väg för teknik- och kompetensutveckling inom stordata, maskininlärning och artificiell intelligens.</P>
<P class="p74 ft19">För att bygga SKA krävs utveckling av tekniskt mycket avancerade komponenter vilket driver innovation i de länder som deltar. Det hittillsvarande svenska engagemanget i SKAO har tagit fasta på detta och etablerat samverkan mellan akademin, forskningsfinansiärer och teknikföretag på ett sätt som är nytt för Sverige. Konkret betyder det att Sveriges bidrag till konstruktionen av SKA till stor del kommer att utgöras av leveranser av tekniskt avancerade komponenter. För att vissa bestämmelser om privilegier och immunitet i konventionen om upprättande av Square Kilometre Array Observatory ska kunna tillämpas i Sverige krävs en ändring i lagen om immunitet och privilegier i vissa fall (se avsnitt 7 och</P>
<P class="p75 ft3">8). Riksdagens godkännande av konventionen krävs därför enligt 10 kap.</P>
<P class="p58 ft3">3 § regeringsformen. Regeringen föreslår att riksdagen godkänner att Sverige tillträder konventionen.</P>

<DIV id="page_12">


<DIV>
<DIV id="id_1">
<P class="p77 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106</P>
<P class="p78 ft3">12</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p79 ft14">Artiklarna 2 och 3</P>
<P class="p80 ft3">Organisationen ska inom ramen för sin officiella verksamhet ha immunitet mot rättsliga förfaranden utom i några specifikt angivna fall, bland annat har organisationen inte immunitet när det gäller kvarstadsbeslut som fattats av administrativa eller rättsliga myndigheter avseende löner och arvoden som SKAO är skyldig en av sina anställda. Vidare ska organisationens lokaler vara okränkbara med vissa undantag såsom vid brand eller annan nödsituation.</P>
<P class="p54 ft14">Artiklarna 4 och 5</P>
<P class="p80 ft3">Inom ramen för sin officiella verksamhet ska SKAO, dess tillgångar, egendom, inkomster, vinster, verksamheter och transaktioner vara befriade från alla direkta skatter, med undantag för den andel som utgör en avgift för specifika tjänster. SKAO ska vara befriat från mervärdesskatt för förvärv av varor och tjänster (inbegripet publikationer, informationsmaterial och motorfordon) som är av betydande värde och nödvändiga för den officiella verksamheten. SKAO ska vidare vara befriat från tullar och skatter, t.ex. mervärdesskatt och punktskatter, på import av varor, inbegripet publikationer, som är av betydande värde, som organisationen importerat för officiell användning. Dock ska ingen befrielse beviljas för tull och indirekta skatter för varor som köpts eller importerats, eller tjänster som tillhandahållits, för personalens personliga bruk.</P>
<P class="p81 ft14">Artikel 6</P>
<P class="p80 ft3">Artikel 6 behandlar återförsäljning av varor och innebär bl.a. att varor som har förvärvats eller importerats enligt artikel 5 inte ska säljas, skänkas bort, hyras ut eller på annat sätt avyttras på en medlemsstats territorium om inte den medlemsstaten i förväg har informerats och eventuella relevanta avgifter och skatter har betalats och eventuella villkor som avtalats med den medlemsstaten har iakttagits.</P>
<P class="p52 ft14">Artikel 7</P>
<P class="p82 ft3">När det gäller privilegier och immunitet för personal gäller enligt artikel 7 i protokollet följande. Generaldirektören och all personal som utför sina uppgifter i en medlemsstat ska, tillsammans med sina familjemedlemmar, om inte denna immunitet i ett visst fall har upphävts, åtnjuta följande privilegier och immunitet:</P>
<P class="p83 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">Immunitet mot rättsliga förfaranden i fråga om alla åtgärder som de vidtar i sin tjänsteutövning, inbegripet muntliga eller skriftliga uttalanden. Denna immunitet ska fortsätta att gälla även efter det att deras anställning vid SKAO har upphört. Immuniteten ska inte gälla för vägtrafikbrott och skada som orsakats av ett fordon som framförts av dem.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p84 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">Samma undantag från åtgärder som begränsar invandring och statlig utlänningsregistrering som i regel beviljas anställda vid internationella organisationer.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p85 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">Undantag från obligatorisk offentlig tjänst.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_13">


<P class="p72 ft3">d) Alla officiella handlingar och dokument som rör utförandet av deras Prop. 2024/25:106 uppgifter inom ramen för SKAO:s officiella verksamhet ska vara okränk-</P>
<P class="p79 ft3">bara.</P>
<P class="p86 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">Löner och arvoden, men inte pension och livränta, som SKAO betalar till sin generaldirektör och personal för deras aktiva tjänst vid SKAO ska vara befriade från inhemsk inkomstskatt.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p86 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">Om SKAO upprättar sitt eget sociala trygghetssystem ska SKAO, dess generaldirektör och personal vara befriade från alla obligatoriska bidrag till inhemska socialförsäkringsorgan, och ska inte ha rätt till sådana förmåner, om inte SKAO och medlemmarna kommit överens om annat.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p86 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">g)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">Rätt att tullfritt importera sina möbler och personliga tillhörigheter när de först tillträder sin tjänst och rätt att när de avslutar sitt uppdrag tullfritt exportera sina möbler och personliga tillhörigheter, i båda fallen med förbehåll för de villkor för tullfri avyttring av varor som importeras till medlemsstaten och de allmänna import- och exportbegränsningar som tillämpas i medlemsstaterna.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p87 ft3">Ingen medlemsstat är dock skyldig att erbjuda sina egna medborgare eller stadigvarande bosatta personer de privilegier och den immunitet som avses i artikel 7 punkterna b, c, e, f och g. Med familj avses enligt definitionen i artikel 1 en persons make eller maka eller partner och underhållsberättigade barn som ingår i personens hushåll.</P>
<P class="p52 ft14">Artikel 8</P>
<P class="p59 ft3">Företrädares privilegier och immunitet behandlas i artikel 8 och innebär att företrädare som utför sina uppgifter i en medlemsstat ska åtnjuta immunitet mot rättsliga förfaranden i fråga om alla åtgärder som de vidtar i sin tjänsteutövning, inbegripet muntliga eller skriftliga uttalanden. Denna immunitet ska fortsätta att gälla även efter det att de upphör att vara en företrädare. Vidare ska alla officiella handlingar och dokument som rör utförandet av företrädarnas uppgifter inom ramen för SKAO:s officiella verksamhet vara okränkbara. Med företrädare avses enligt definitionen i artikel 1 företrädare för medlemmarna som deltar i möten i SKAO:s organ eller kommittéer och som omfattar utsedda delegater, suppleanter, rådgivare och sekreterare för delegationer.</P>
<P class="p54 ft14">Artikel 9</P>
<P class="p59 ft3">Beträffande experter gäller enligt artikel 9 att experters alla officiella handlingar och dokument ska vara okränkbara i den utsträckning som behövs för att experterna ska kunna utföra sina uppgifter för SKAO:s räkning inbegripet under tjänsteresor. Med expert avses enligt definitionen i artikel 1 en person som SKAO utser att tjänstgöra vid SKAO under en fastställd tidsperiod.</P>
<P class="p52 ft14">Artikel 10</P>
<P class="p59 ft3">Artikel 10 behandlar samarbete med medlemsstaternas myndigheter och föreskriver bl.a. att alla personer som åtnjuter privilegier och immunitet enligt artiklarna 7, 8 och 9 är skyldiga att följa lagar och förordningar i den medlemsstat i vilken de officiellt verkar.</P>
<P class="p88 ft3">13</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_14">
<DIV id="p14dimg1">
<INGENBILD zsrc="HC0310614x1.jpg/" id="p14img1">
</DIV>


<DIV id="id_1">
<P class="p79 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106 <SPAN class="ft14">Artikel 11</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p79 ft3">14</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p89 ft3">I artikel 11 anges slutligen att privilegier och immunitet som beviljas personer enligt protokollet inte beviljas för dessa personers personliga vinning. De har som enda syfte att säkerställa att SKAO obehindrat kan utföra sina uppgifter och att de personer som beviljats privilegier och immunitet kan agera fullständigt oberoende.</P>
<P class="p90 ft20"><SPAN class="ft1">8</SPAN><SPAN class="ft26">Lagen om immunitet och privilegier i vissa fall bör ändras som en följd av att Sverige tillträder konventionen</SPAN></P>
<P class="p91 ft3"><SPAN class="ft14">Regeringens förslag: </SPAN>Immunitet och privilegier ska gälla för Square Kilometre Array Observatory och medlemmarnas representanter i organet, generaldirektören, organets personal och deras familjemedlemmar samt experter som är utsedda av organet i enlighet med vad som följer av konventionen om upprättande av Square Array Kilometre Observatory.</P>
<P class="p92 ft3"><SPAN class="ft14">Skälen för regeringens förslag: </SPAN>För att konventionens bestämmelser om immunitet och privilegier ska bli gällande inför svenska domstolar och myndigheter måste de införlivas med svensk rätt. Bestämmelser om immunitet och privilegier för internationella organ och personer med anknytning till sådana organ finns i lagen (1976:661) om immunitet och privilegier i vissa fall. I en bilaga till den lagen anges de internationella organ och personer med anknytning till sådana organ som åtnjuter immunitet och privilegier enligt vad som bestäms i stadga eller avtal som är i kraft i förhållande till Sverige. Immuniteten och privilegierna gäller i den utsträckning som framgår av tillämplig internationell överenskommelse.</P>
<P class="p93 ft3">För att bestämmelserna om privilegier och immunitet i konventionen om upprättande av Square Kilometre Array Observatory ska kunna tillämpas i Sverige krävs således en ändring i lagen om immunitet och privilegier i vissa fall. Regeringen föreslår en sådan ändring.</P>
<P class="p94 ft1"><SPAN class="ft1">9</SPAN><SPAN class="ft23">Ikraftträdande</SPAN></P>
<P class="p95 ft3"><SPAN class="ft14">Regeringens förslag: </SPAN>Lagändringen ska träda i kraft den dag som regeringen bestämmer.</P>
<P class="p96 ft3"><SPAN class="ft14">Skälen för regeringens förslag: </SPAN>Konventionen ska vara föremål för ratificering, godtagande eller godkännande av de stater som anges i konventionen (bland andra Sverige) i enlighet med deras inhemska krav. För stater som deponerar sitt <NOBR>ratifikations-,</NOBR> <NOBR>godtagande-,</NOBR> godkännande- eller anslutningsinstrument efter det att konventionen har trätt i kraft ska konventionen träda i kraft trettio dagar efter den dag då dess <NOBR>ratifikations-,</NOBR> godta-</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_15">
<DIV id="p15dimg1">
<INGENBILD zsrc="HC0310615x1.jpg/" id="p15img1">
</DIV>


<P class="p97 ft3"><NOBR>gande-,</NOBR> godkännande- eller anslutningsinstrument deponerades. Med hän- Prop. 2024/25:106 syn till att det inte redan nu säkert kan anges när konventionen blir bin-</P>
<P class="p98 ft3">dande för Sverige bör den föreslagna lagändringen träda i kraft den dag som regeringen bestämmer.</P>
<P class="p99 ft1"><SPAN class="ft1">10</SPAN><SPAN class="ft27">Ekonomiska konsekvenser</SPAN></P>
<P class="p100 ft3">Några direkta offentligfinansiella effekter bedöms inte följa av avtalet. Kostnaderna för att genomföra förslagen i denna proposition bedöms kunna hanteras inom befintliga anslagsramar.</P>

<P class="p101 ft21">Förslaget till lag om ändring i lagen (1976:661) om immunitet och privilegier i vissa fall</P>

	<TD colspan=2 class="tr6 td71"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">ganisationens</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr6 td38"><SPAN class="p14 ft3">inter-</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>

	<TD class="tr7 td24"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>

	<TD class="tr7 td24"><SPAN class="p3 ft4">Array Observatory</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD colspan=4 class="tr7 td24"><SPAN class="p3 ft4">resentanter i organet,</SPAN> </TD>

	<TD colspan=2 class="tr6 td75"><SPAN class="p40 ft4">Kilometre</SPAN> </TD>

	<TD colspan=2 class="tr7 td68"><SPAN class="p39 ft4">familje-</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD colspan=3 class="tr7 td43"><SPAN class="p3 ft4">Array Observatory</SPAN> </TD>

<P class="p108 ft4">medlemmar samt experter utsedda av organet</P>
<P class="p109 ft3">Bilagan innehåller bestämmelser om vilka organ och personer med anknytning till sådana organ som har immunitet och privilegier enligt avtal.</P>
<P class="p110 ft3">15</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_16">


<DIV>
<DIV id="id_1">
<P class="p79 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106</P>
<P class="p111 ft3">16</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p112 ft3"><SPAN class="ft4">Punkt 85</SPAN>, som är ny, innebär att konventionens bestämmelser om privilegier och immunitet för Square Kilometre Array Observatory och medlemmarnas representanter i organet, generaldirektören, organets personal och deras familjemedlemmar samt av organet utsedda experter införlivas i svensk rätt. Immuniteten och privilegierna gäller i den utsträckning som framgår av konventionen.</P>
<P class="p113 ft3">Övervägandena finns i avsnitt 8.</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_17">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p79 ft1">Convention establishing the Square Kilometre Array Observatory</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p79 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106 Bilaga 1</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p114 ft3">The Parties to this Convention,</P>
<P class="p115 ft3">DESIRING to deliver one of the most visionary and ambitious science projects of the 21st century involving significant international cooperation;</P>
<P class="p116 ft3">COMMITTED to testing the limits of engineering and scientific endeavour and to exploring fundamental questions in astronomy and physics;</P>
<P class="p116 ft3">NOTING that the Square Kilometre Array will be a next generation radio telescope facility that has a discovery potential far greater than any previous instrument;</P>
<P class="p116 ft3">RECOGNISING that the scale and ambition of the Square Kilometre Array demand a global effort with <NOBR>long-term</NOBR> investment;</P>
<P class="p117 ft3">EMBRACING the potential for scientific discovery to contribute to advances in technology and innovation and to deliver a broader benefit for industry and society;</P>
<P class="p116 ft3">DEDICATED to realising the full ambition of the Square Kilometre Array Project;</P>
<P class="p117 ft3">ACKNOWLEDGING the preparatory work done by the Square Kilometre Array Organisation in the establishment of the Square Kilometre Array Observatory;</P>
<P class="p116 ft3">COMMITTED to an organisation where diversity and equality are promoted and respected;</P>
<P class="p118 ft3">HAVE AGREED as follows:</P>
<P class="p119 ft3">17</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_18">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p79 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106 Bilaga 1</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p120 ft3">Article 1</P>
<P class="p121 ft3">Definitions</P>
<P class="p122 ft3">For the purposes of this Convention and its Protocols:</P>
<P class="p122 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">“SKAO” means the Square Kilometre Array Observatory;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p123 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">“SKA” means the Square Kilometre Array radio telescope facility;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p124 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">“SKA Project” means the global effort to build, maintain, operate and ultimately decommission the SKA;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p85 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(d)</SPAN><NOBR><SPAN class="ft25">“SKA-1”</SPAN></NOBR> means the initial phase of the SKA Project;</P>
<P class="p125 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">“Headquarters Country” means the State in which the SKAO global headquarters is located;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p85 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">“Host Country” means a State in which the SKA Project is hosted;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p124 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(g)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">“Member” means a State or an international organisation that is a party to this Convention;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p126 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(h)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">“Associate Member” means a State or an international organisation that is not a party to this Convention and which is admitted to the SKAO in accordance with Article 6, paragraph 3;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p83 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(i)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">“Fair Work Return” is identified to have been achieved when the cumulative value of the goods, works and services provided by a Member through the procurement process, broadly reflects the financial contribution committed by that Member;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p127 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(j)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">“Official Activities” means all activities undertaken pursuant to the Convention including the SKAO’s administrative activities;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p85 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(k)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">“Staff” means members of staff of, or secondees to, the SKAO; and</SPAN></P>
<P class="p128 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(l)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">“Funding Schedule” means a schedule that prescribes financial contributions, and terms and conditions, of Members and Associate Members for the construction and operation of the SKAO.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p129 ft3">Article 2</P>
<P class="p130 ft3">Establishment and Status of the SKAO</P>
<P class="p131 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">The SKAO is hereby established as an international organisation with legal personality. It shall have such capacities as may be necessary for the exercise of its functions and fulfilment of its purposes, including:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p85 ft3">(a) To contract;</P>
<P class="p123 ft3">(b) To acquire and dispose of immovable and movable property; and</P>
<P class="p85 ft3">(c) To institute and be a party to legal proceedings.</P>
<P class="p132 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">The Headquarters Country shall be the United Kingdom of Great Britain and Northern Ireland, and the global headquarters of the SKAO shall be at Jodrell Bank.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p133 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">The SKAO shall conclude agreements with the Headquarters Country and Host Countries concerning the hosting of the SKAO and the SKA Project. Such agreements shall be approved by unanimous vote of the Council.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p79 ft3">18</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_19">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t15">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr10 td35"><SPAN class="p134 ft3">Article 3</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr10 td13"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr14 td35"><SPAN class="p3 ft30">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr14 td13"><SPAN class="p3 ft13">Bilaga 1</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr7 td35"><SPAN class="p135 ft3">Purpose of the SKAO</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr7 td13"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p136 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">The purpose of the SKAO shall be to facilitate and promote a global collaboration in radio astronomy with a view to the delivery of transformational science. The first objective of this global collaboration shall be the implementation of the SKA Project.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p137 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">Subject to a decision by the Council, the SKAO may commence, or contribute to, other projects, beyond the SKA Project, that are related to radio astronomy science, technology and their applications. Participation by Members and Associate Members in such other projects shall be optional.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p138 ft3">Article 4</P>
<P class="p139 ft3">Privileges and Immunities</P>
<P class="p140 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">All Members shall grant the privileges and immunities as set out in the Protocol on Privileges and Immunities of the Square Kilometre Array Observatory, which shall be annexed to (Annex A), and form an integral part of, this Convention.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p137 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">All privileges and immunities are provided for the sole purpose of facilitating the Official Activities of the SKAO and delivery of its objectives.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p141 ft3">Article 5</P>
<P class="p142 ft3">SKA Project</P>
<P class="p136 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">The SKA Project shall be designed to be capable of transformational science, with a combination of sensitivity, angular resolution, and survey speed far surpassing current </SPAN><NOBR>state-of-the-art</NOBR> instruments at relevant radio frequencies.</P>
<P class="p143 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">The SKA Project shall be delivered in phases, beginning with SKA- 1, with the active intent to proceed to subsequent phases.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p136 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><NOBR><SPAN class="ft5">SKA-1</SPAN></NOBR> shall be hosted in Australia and the Republic of South Africa. The components of <NOBR>SKA-1</NOBR> to be located in each Host Country, and components of the global headquarters of the SKAO to be located in the Headquarters Country, shall be described in a technical document to be approved by unanimous decision of the Council.</P>
<P class="p137 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">Subsequent phases of the SKA Project shall commence following approval by decision of the Council. Participation in the construction of such subsequent phases shall be optional. Financial contributions towards the implementation of a subsequent phase shall be determined in</SPAN></P>
<P class="p144 ft3">19</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_20">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p79 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106 Bilaga 1</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p145 ft3">accordance with the Financial Protocol of the Square Kilometre Array Observatory.</P>
<P class="p146 ft3">Article 6</P>
<P class="p147 ft3">Membership and Other Forms of Cooperation</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p148 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">The Parties to this Convention shall be the Members of the SKAO. Membership shall be open to States and international organisations.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p149 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">The Council may decide, by unanimous vote, to admit new Members into the SKAO in accordance with this Convention and on such terms as it determines. When the Convention enters into force for that State or international organisation according to Article 19, paragraph 4, it shall become a Member and shall be bound by the terms determined by the Council.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p149 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">The Council may decide, by unanimous vote, to admit Associate Members to the SKAO on such terms as it determines. Such terms shall ensure that Associate Members do not enjoy benefits equivalent to those of Members. Associate membership shall be open to States and international organisations.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p149 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">The Council may decide, by unanimous vote, to invite other entities such as States, international organisations, and institutions, to cooperate with the SKAO. The SKAO may enter into agreements and arrangements with them to this effect. These agreements and arrangements require the approval by decision of the Council.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p150 ft3">Article 7</P>
<P class="p151 ft3">Organs</P>
<P class="p152 ft3">The SKAO shall consist of the Council and a <NOBR>Director-General</NOBR> assisted by Staff.</P>
<P class="p153 ft3">Article 8</P>
<P class="p154 ft3">Council</P>
<P class="p155 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">The Council shall be the governing body of the SKAO. Each Member shall be represented on the Council by up to two representatives, one of whom shall be the voting representative who shall be authorised to act and vote on its behalf. Representatives may be assisted by advisers.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p156 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">The Council shall be responsible for the overall strategic and scientific direction of the SKAO, its good governance, and the attainment of its purposes. It shall have all necessary and proper authority to discharge effectively its responsibilities.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p157 ft3">20</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_21">


<DIV>
<DIV id="id_1">
<P class="p158 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">In addition to the functions set forth elsewhere in this Convention, the Council shall:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p159 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">Appoint the </SPAN><NOBR>Director-General</NOBR> and approve the appointment of other senior staff, as required in accordance with the Staff Regulations;</P>
<P class="p160 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">Approve the policies, rules, and regulations of the SKAO, including with regard to scientific, technical, financial and administrative matters, as well as access to the SKA and its data;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p123 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">Approve the budget and supervise expenditure and financial activity;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p85 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">Appoint auditors;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p123 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">Approve and publish the audited annual accounts;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p85 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">Approve and publish annual reports; and</SPAN></P>
<P class="p158 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(g)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">Take further measures, as necessary for the functioning of the SKAO.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p161 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">For any meeting, convened either in person or remotely, and for any decision of the Council a quorum of </SPAN><NOBR>two-thirds</NOBR> of Members shall be required. Members not eligible to vote shall not be considered part of the quorum.</P>
<P class="p162 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">Each Member shall have one vote in the Council, unless otherwise specified.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p159 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">Decisions by the Council shall be taken by a vote of a </SPAN><NOBR>two-thirds</NOBR> majority, unless otherwise specified.</P>
<P class="p161 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">7.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">In determining the unanimity or majorities provided for in this Convention or the Financial Protocol of the Square Kilometre Array Observatory, account shall not be taken of a Member which is absent, is not participating in the vote, abstains or has no right to vote.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p161 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">8.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">The choice of the Headquarters Country and each Host Country may be amended, subject to Article 15, after a unanimous vote of the Council.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p161 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">9.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">For projects approved in accordance with Article 3, paragraph 2, Members shall not have the right to vote unless they have agreed to make a financial contribution.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p162 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">10.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">Subject to the terms of this Convention, the Council shall determine its own Rules of Procedure.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p161 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">11.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">The Council shall elect a Chairperson and </SPAN><NOBR>Vice-Chairperson</NOBR> for a term of office of two years. The Chairperson and <NOBR>Vice-Chairperson</NOBR> may not be elected more than twice.</P>
<P class="p161 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">12.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">The Chairperson shall convene the meetings of the Council in accordance with its Rules of Procedure. The Council shall meet as and when required, but not less than once per year.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p161 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">13.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">The Council shall establish a Finance Committee on which every Member shall be represented. The Council shall establish such other</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p47 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106 Bilaga 1</P>
<P class="p163 ft3">21</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_22">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p79 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106 Bilaga 1</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p164 ft3">committees as may be necessary to accomplish the purpose of the SKAO. The Council shall define the mandate and membership of such committees.</P>
<P class="p165 ft3">Article 9</P>
<P class="p166 ft3"><NOBR>Director-General</NOBR> and Staff</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p167 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">The Council shall appoint a </SPAN><NOBR>Director-General</NOBR> for a fixed period and may terminate the appointment at any time in accordance with Staff Regulations to be approved, by decision, by the Council. The Director- General shall act as the chief executive officer of the SKAO and act as its legal representative. The <NOBR>Director-General</NOBR> shall report to the Council.</P>
<P class="p168 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">The functions of the </SPAN><NOBR>Director-General</NOBR> shall be to:</P>
<P class="p169 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">Exercise project, operational and financial authority as provided by the Council;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p170 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">Submit an annual report to the Council;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p171 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">Submit budget estimates to the Council;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p170 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">Submit audited annual accounts to the Council;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p172 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft31">Attend Council meetings in a consultative capacity unless the Council otherwise decides;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p170 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">Be responsible for general management of SKAO;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p171 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(g)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">Be accountable for health and safety; and</SPAN></P>
<P class="p171 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(h)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">Perform all other duties as delegated by the Council.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p156 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">Subject to Article 8, paragraph 3 (a), the </SPAN><NOBR>Director-General</NOBR> shall be assisted by such scientific, technical, and administrative staff as the <NOBR>Director-General</NOBR> may consider necessary within the limits authorised by the Council. Such staff shall be engaged and dismissed by the Director- General in accordance with the Staff Regulations.</P>
<P class="p149 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft8">The </SPAN><NOBR>Director-General</NOBR> and Staff shall respect the international character of the SKAO and perform their duties in the sole interests of the SKAO.</P>
<P class="p173 ft3">Article 10</P>
<P class="p174 ft3">Financial Matters</P>
<P class="p175 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">The SKAO shall conduct its financial affairs in accordance with the Financial Protocol of the Square Kilometre Array Observatory, which shall be annexed to (Annex B), and form an integral part of, this Convention.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p156 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">Members and Associate Members shall make financial contributions in accordance with Funding Schedules that have been approved by the Council in accordance with the Financial Protocol of the Square Kilometre Array Observatory.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p157 ft3">22</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_23">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t16">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr10 td76"><SPAN class="p176 ft3">3. The Funding Schedules may be amended in accordance with the</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr10 td13"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr6 td76"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">Financial Protocol of the Square Kilometre Array Observatory.</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr6 td13"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">Bilaga 1</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p177 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">Members and Associate Members shall have shares in the SKA Project proportional to their cumulative committed financial contributions to the SKA Project.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p178 ft3">Article 11</P>
<P class="p179 ft3">Intellectual Property Rights</P>
<P class="p177 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">The SKAO shall have an Intellectual Property Policy, approved by the Council by unanimous vote. Any amendment by the Council of the Intellectual Property Policy shall require a </SPAN><NOBR>two-thirds</NOBR> majority, except for those provisions that have been identified in the policy as requiring unanimity to be amended.</P>
<P class="p180 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">The policy shall ensure that intellectual property is managed to minimise intellectual </SPAN><NOBR>property-related</NOBR> risk and cost to the SKAO.</P>
<P class="p181 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">The policy shall define the basis on which any entities that participate in projects undertaken by the SKAO are able to exploit, beyond the scope of the SKA, any innovations that arise from their participation.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p177 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">The Council may decide to grant access to foreground intellectual property through the grant of </SPAN><NOBR>non-exclusive,</NOBR> worldwide, <NOBR>royalty-free,</NOBR> perpetual, and irrevocable <NOBR>sub-licences</NOBR> to SKA contributors, under which they will be permitted to use those innovation and work products, subject to obtaining appropriate licences under existing background intellectual property rights and third party intellectual property rights, for SKA Project purposes and other <NOBR>non-commercial</NOBR> research and education purposes, provided that such <NOBR>sub-licences</NOBR> should not cover activities undertaken by <NOBR>sub-licensees</NOBR> in competition with the owner of the foreground intellectual property.</P>
<P class="p182 ft3">Article 12</P>
<P class="p183 ft3">Procurement</P>
<P class="p177 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">The primary objective of procurement shall be to acquire successfully the goods, works and services required to deliver the SKA Project through financial contributions, whether cash or </SPAN><NOBR>in-kind</NOBR> contributions or a combination of both, while effectively managing risk.</P>
<P class="p184 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">A Procurement Policy shall be approved by the Council by unanimous vote. Any amendment by the Council of the Procurement Policy shall require a </SPAN><NOBR>two-thirds</NOBR> majority, except for those provisions that have been identified in the policy as requiring unanimity to be amended.</P>
<P class="p122 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">Procurement shall be implemented based on principles of Fair Work</SPAN></P>
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t17">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr6 td77"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">Return, equity, transparency and competitiveness.</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr6 td78"><SPAN class="p14 ft3">23</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_24">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t18">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr10 td79"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr10 td80"><SPAN class="p185 ft3">Article 13</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr6 td79"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">Bilaga 1</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr6 td80"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr7 td79"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr7 td80"><SPAN class="p185 ft19">Operations and Access</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p156 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">The SKAO shall conduct its operations in accordance with the Operations Policy, as approved by the Council by unanimous vote. Any amendment by the Council of the Operations Policy shall require a twothirds majority, except for those provisions that have been identified in the policy as requiring unanimity to be amended.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p149 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">Access to time on SKA telescopes and other SKA resources shall be in accordance with the Access Policy, as approved by the Council by unanimous vote. Any amendment by the Council of the Access Policy shall require a </SPAN><NOBR>two-thirds</NOBR> majority, except for those provisions that have been identified in the policy as requiring unanimity to be amended.</P>
<P class="p186 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">The SKAO will operate on the principle that Members’ and Associate Members’ access is proportional to their share in the project, except as decided by unanimous vote of the Council.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p187 ft3">Article 14</P>
<P class="p188 ft3">Dispute Settlement</P>
<P class="p156 ft3">Any dispute arising between Members or between a Member, or Members, and the SKAO with regard to the interpretation or application of this Convention which cannot be settled by negotiation shall, at the request of any of the parties to the dispute, be referred to the Permanent Court of Arbitration under the relevant Arbitration Rules of the Permanent Court of Arbitration, unless the parties to the dispute have agreed to another mode of settlement.</P>
<P class="p189 ft3">Article 15</P>
<P class="p190 ft3">Amendments</P>
<P class="p156 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">Any Member wishing to propose an amendment to this Convention and its Protocols shall notify the </SPAN><NOBR>Director-General</NOBR> of its proposal. The <NOBR>Director-General</NOBR> shall promptly circulate any such proposals to all Members. Following a subsequent period of at least three months the Chairperson shall convene a meeting of the Council at which it shall consider whether to adopt and recommend the amendment to Members.</P>
<P class="p149 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">Amendments adopted and recommended by the Council shall enter into force for all Members after all Members have accepted them in accordance with their own domestic requirements. Such amendments shall enter into force thirty days after the last notification of acceptance of the proposed amendment has been received by the depositary.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p191 ft3">24</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_25">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t19">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr10 td81"><SPAN class="p192 ft3">Article 16</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr10 td13"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr14 td81"><SPAN class="p3 ft30">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr14 td13"><SPAN class="p3 ft13">Bilaga 1</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr7 td81"><SPAN class="p193 ft3">Withdrawal</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr7 td13"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p136 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">Ten years after the date this Convention enters into force any Member may at any time withdraw from this Convention, by giving written notice of its withdrawal to the depositary. Withdrawal shall be allowed on the condition that the withdrawing Member has fulfilled its obligations, unless the Council decides to waive such obligations.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p137 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft31">A withdrawing Member shall remain liable for all direct and contingent obligations to the SKAO to which it was subject on the date the withdrawal notice was received by the depositary, until the point at which the withdrawal becomes effective. So long as the withdrawing Member has fulfilled its obligations, withdrawal shall become effective twelve months after the withdrawal notice was received, unless the Council decides that earlier withdrawal should be permitted.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p194 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">A withdrawing Member shall have no claim on the assets of the SKAO or on the amount of the financial contributions it has already made. A withdrawing Member shall not incur any new liability for obligations resulting from operations of the SKAO effected after the date on which the withdrawal notice is received by the depository.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p195 ft3">Article 17</P>
<P class="p196 ft3">Termination and Dissolution</P>
<P class="p140 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">The Council may decide, by a unanimous vote, to terminate this Convention at any time. Termination shall not take effect until such time as the SKAO’s obligations to the Host Countries, including in relation to the decommissioning of the SKA, have been discharged. Once discharged, the Council shall decide the date upon which termination will take effect. Upon termination, the SKAO shall be dissolved and cease to exist as an International Organisation. Any assets shall be liquidated and any proceeds distributed among Members pro rata to the contributions they have made since becoming Members.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p197 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">Any outstanding liabilities incurred by SKAO shall be borne by Members pro rata to, and to the extent of, the financial contributions they have been required to provide the SKAO since becoming Members as at the time of the decision to terminate. In case that the obligations or liabilities incurred by SKAO exceed total funds then available to SKAO, the Council shall, by unanimous decision, seek to increase each Member’s contribution for such obligation or liability.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p198 ft3">25</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_26">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p79 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106 Bilaga 1</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p199 ft3">Article 18</P>
<P class="p200 ft3">Failure to Fulfil Obligations</P>
<P class="p201 ft19">When the Council decides that a Member has failed to fulfil its obligations arising out of this Convention, including the payment of financial contributions, it shall be called upon by the Council to rectify the failure. If the said Member does not respond to the Council’s request in the time imparted to it, the Council voting rights of that Member shall be automatically suspended. The other Members of the Council may decide to take such other action as they consider appropriate in the circumstances, which may include a unanimous decision of the other Members of the Council that the Member ceases to be a Member of the SKAO.</P>
<P class="p202 ft3">Article 19</P>
<P class="p203 ft3">Signature, Ratification, Acceptance, Approval, Accession and Entry into Force</P>
<P class="p204 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">This Convention shall be open for signature in Rome on [a date to be determined by the Presidency] and thereafter with the Depositary from [a date to be determined by the Presidency and the Depositary] for all States listed below:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p205 ft3">Australia</P>
<P class="p123 ft3">The People’s Republic of China</P>
<P class="p85 ft3">India</P>
<P class="p123 ft3">Italy</P>
<P class="p123 ft3">The Kingdom of the Netherlands</P>
<P class="p85 ft3">New Zealand</P>
<P class="p123 ft3">The Portuguese Republic</P>
<P class="p123 ft3">Kingdom of Sweden</P>
<P class="p85 ft3">Republic of South Africa</P>
<P class="p123 ft3">United Kingdom of Great Britain and Northern Ireland</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p206 ft3">2. This Convention shall be subject to ratification, acceptance or approval by the States listed in paragraph 1 in accordance with their domestic requirements. It shall enter into force thirty days after the date on which instruments of ratification, acceptance or approval have been deposited by Australia, the Republic of South Africa, United Kingdom of</P>

<DIV id="id_1">
<P class="p199 ft3">Article 20</P>
<P class="p208 ft3">Depositary</P>
<P class="p159 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft31">The Government of the United Kingdom of Great Britain and Northern Ireland shall be the depositary for this Convention.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p122 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">The depositary shall:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p158 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">Notify signatories and Members of each signature and the date thereof, and the date of entry into force of this Convention;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p160 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">Notify signatories and Members of each deposit of instruments of ratification, acceptance, approval or accession and the date of entry into force of the Convention for that State or international organisation;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p209 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">Inform the Members of the dates of notifications of acceptance and of the date of the entry into force of an amendment;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p209 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">Inform the Members of the date of a withdrawal notice and of the date the withdrawal takes effect;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p85 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">Inform the Members of the date of termination of the Convention;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p79 ft3">and</P>
<P class="p210 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">Inform the Members of a decision of the Council, in accordance with Article 18, that a Member ceases to be a Member of the SKAO and of the date that decision takes effect.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p211 ft3">3.Upon the entry into force of this Convention, the depositary shall register it with the Secretariat of the United Nations in accordance with Article 102 of the Charter of the United Nations.</P>

	<TD class="tr13 td90"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">The Parties to the Convention have agreed as follows:</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr13 td13"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>

<TR>
	<TD class="tr13 td90"><SPAN class="p219 ft3">Article 1</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr13 td13"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr23 td90"><SPAN class="p221 ft3">Definitions</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr23 td13"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p147 ft3">For the purposes of this Protocol:</P>
<P class="p222 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">“Expert” means a person named by the SKAO as being in the service of the SKAO for a defined period of time;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p223 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft32">“Family” means, with respect to any person, the spouse or partner and dependent children forming part of such a person’s household;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p224 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">“Premises” means sites, buildings and facilities or parts thereof, irrespective of ownership, that are occupied exclusively by the SKAO for the performance of its Official Activities;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p225 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft33">“Representatives” means representatives of the Members in attendance at meetings of organs or committees of the SKAO and includes designated delegates, alternates, advisors and secretaries of delegations;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p224 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft34">“Archives” means correspondence, documents, manuscripts, photographs, films, recordings, computer and media data, data carriers and any other similar material belonging to or held by the SKAO and all the information contained therein; and</SPAN></P>
<P class="p222 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">“Immunity from legal process” means immunity from jurisdiction and immunity from execution measures.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p141 ft3">Article 2</P>
<P class="p226 ft3">Immunity from Legal Process</P>
<P class="p143 ft3">Within the scope of its Official Activities, the SKAO shall have Immunity from legal process except:</P>
<P class="p223 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">To the extent that by a decision of the Council the SKAO waives it in a particular case;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p224 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">In respect of a civil action by a third party for damage arising from an accident caused by a vehicle belonging to or operated on behalf of the SKAO or in respect of a traffic offence;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p222 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">In respect of an arbitration award made under Article 14 of the Convention;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p224 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">In the event of an attachment order, pursuant to a decision by the administrative or judicial authorities, of the salaries, wages and emoluments owed by the SKAO to a member of its Staff; and</SPAN></P>
<P class="p222 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">In respect of a counter claim relating directly to a main claim brought by the SKAO.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p227 ft3">29</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_30">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p79 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106 Bilaga 1</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p120 ft3">Article 3</P>
<P class="p228 ft3">The Premises</P>
<P class="p83 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">The Premises shall be inviolable. Any person having the authority to enter any place under any legal provision shall not exercise that authority in respect of the Premises unless permission to do so has been given by the DirectorGeneral or by the head of the Premises designated by the Director- General and acting on the </SPAN><NOBR>Director-General’s</NOBR> behalf.</P>
<P class="p83 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">Such permission may be presumed in the event of fire or other emergencies requiring prompt protective action. Any person who has entered the Premises with the presumed permission of the Director- General or by the Head of the Premises shall, if so requested by the </SPAN><NOBR>Director-General</NOBR> or by the Head of the Premises, leave the Premises immediately.</P>
<P class="p229 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">The </SPAN><NOBR>Director-General</NOBR> shall notify each relevant Member State of the names of Heads of Premises located within its jurisdiction.</P>
<P class="p128 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">The SKAO shall not allow its Premises to be used for any unlawful activity or to act as a haven or refuge to any person facing any judicial or administrative procedures in a Member State.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p127 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">The Archives wherever they may be located and by whomsoever held shall be inviolable at all times.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p165 ft3">Article 4</P>
<P class="p230 ft3">Exemption from Direct Taxation</P>
<P class="p231 ft3">Within the scope of its Official Activities, the SKAO, its assets, property, income, gains, operations and transactions shall be exempt from all direct taxes, with the exception of the proportion which represents a charge for specific services rendered.</P>
<P class="p165 ft3">Article 5</P>
<P class="p232 ft3">Exemption from Customs and Indirect Taxes</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p167 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">The SKAO shall be exempted from value added tax in respect of goods and services (including publications, information material and motor vehicles), which are of substantial value and necessary for Official Activities. The exemption may be provided at the point of sale or through a subsequent reimbursement, consistent with the relevant practice followed by each Member State. Restrictions on the number of motor vehicles exempt from value added tax may be applied, consistent with a</SPAN></P>
<P class="p233 ft3">Member State’s domestic legislation and policy.</P>
<P class="p234 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">The SKAO shall be exempted from duties (whether of customs or excise) and taxes on the importation of goods, including publications, which are of substantial value, imported by it for its official use.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p235 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">Such exemptions shall be subject to compliance with such conditions as the Member State may prescribe, including for the protection of the revenue and import or export controls.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p236 ft3">30</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_31">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t25">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr10 td76"><SPAN class="p237 ft3">4. No exemption shall be granted under this Article in respect of goods</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr10 td13"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr6 td76"><SPAN class="p237 ft3">purchased or imported, or services provided, for the personal benefit of</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr6 td13"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">Bilaga 1</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr6 td76"><SPAN class="p238 ft3">Staff.</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr6 td13"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p224 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft8">National laws and regulations concerning the importation and exportation of goods and services continue to apply in all other aspects, including biosecurity and quarantine laws and regulations.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p222 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">Member States may exempt any </SPAN><NOBR>in-kind</NOBR> contributions they make to the SKAO from value added tax.</P>
<P class="p141 ft3">Article 6</P>
<P class="p239 ft3">Resale of Goods</P>
<P class="p140 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">Goods which have been acquired or imported under Article 5 shall not be sold, given away, hired out or otherwise disposed of in the territory of a Member State unless that Member State has been informed beforehand and any relevant duties and taxes have been paid and any conditions agreed with that Member State have been complied with.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p240 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">The duties and taxes to be paid shall be calculated by the Member State on the basis of the rates prevailing and the value of the goods on the date at the time of disposal. The Member State shall provide the SKAO with the necessary instructions regarding the procedure to be followed.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p138 ft3">Article 7</P>
<P class="p241 ft3">Privileges and Immunities of Staff including the <NOBR>Director-General</NOBR></P>
<P class="p136 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">The </SPAN><NOBR>Director-General</NOBR> and all Staff who discharge their functions in a Member State shall, together with members of their Family, and except to the extent that in any particular case such immunity has been waived by the competent authority set out in Article 11, enjoy the following privileges and immunities:</P>
<P class="p242 ft3">a) Immunity from legal process in respect of all acts performed by them in their official capacity, including their words spoken or written. This immunity shall continue to be accorded even after the termination of their employment with the SKAO. This immunity shall not apply to road traffic offences and damage resulting from a vehicle driven by them;</P>
<P class="p224 ft3">b) The same exemptions from measures restricting immigration and government aliens’ registration that are generally accorded to members of personnel of international organisations;</P>
<P class="p243 ft3">c) Exemption from compulsory public service;</P>
<P class="p224 ft3">d) Inviolability of all their official papers and documents related to the exercise of their function within the scope of the Official Activities of the SKAO;</P>
<P class="p224 ft3">e) Salaries and emoluments, but not pensions and annuities, paid by SKAO to its <NOBR>Director-General</NOBR> and Staff in respect of their active service with SKAO shall be exempt from domestic income tax;</P>
<P class="p224 ft3">f) In the event that it establishes its own social security scheme, the SKAO, its <NOBR>Director-General</NOBR> and Staff shall be exempt from all compulsory contributions to domestic social security bodies, and shall not be entitled</P>
<P class="p244 ft3">31</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_32">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p79 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106 Bilaga 1</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p145 ft3">to such benefits, subject to agreement between the SKAO and Members; and</P>
<P class="p112 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">g)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">The right to import </SPAN><NOBR>duty-free</NOBR> their furniture and personal effects (including at least one motor vehicle) at the time of first taking up their post and the right on the termination of their functions to export <NOBR>duty-free</NOBR> their furniture and personal effects, subject in both cases to the conditions governing the disposal of goods imported into the Member State <NOBR>duty-free</NOBR> and to the general restrictions applied in Member States to imports and exports.</P>
<P class="p245 ft3">2. No Member State is obliged to extend the privileges and immunities referred to in the present Article, paragraph 1(b), (c), (e), (f) and (g), to its own nationals or permanent residents.</P>
<P class="p165 ft3">Article 8</P>
<P class="p246 ft3">Privileges and Immunities of Representatives</P>
<P class="p231 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">Representatives who discharge their functions in a Member State shall, and except to the extent that in any particular case such immunity has been waived by the competent authority set out in Article 11, enjoy the following privileges and immunities:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p83 ft3">a) Immunity from legal process in respect of all acts performed by them in their official capacity, including their words spoken or written. This immunity shall continue to be accorded even after they cease to be a Representative. This immunity shall not apply to road traffic offences and damage resulting from a vehicle driven by them;</P>
<P class="p247 ft3">b) Inviolability of all their official papers and documents related to the exercise of their function within the scope of the Official Activities of the SKAO; and</P>
<P class="p126 ft3">c) Member States shall take measures to facilitate the free movement of Representatives in the exercise of their functions, in accordance with domestic law.</P>
<P class="p248 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft31">The SKAO shall provide suitable accreditation or authorisation documentation to Representatives.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p128 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">No Member State is obliged to extend the privileges and immunities referred to in the present Article, paragraph 1 (c), to its own nationals or permanent residents.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p129 ft3">Article 9</P>
<P class="p249 ft3">Experts</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p167 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">Experts shall enjoy inviolability for all their official papers and documents to the extent necessary for the carrying out of their functions on behalf of the SKAO, including during journeys made in carrying out their functions.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p250 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">Member States shall take measures to facilitate the free movement of Experts in the exercise of their functions, in accordance with domestic law.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p251 ft3">32</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_33">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t26">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr10 td91"><SPAN class="p252 ft3">Article 10</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr10 td13"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr14 td91"><SPAN class="p3 ft30">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr14 td13"><SPAN class="p3 ft13">Bilaga 1</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr7 td91"><SPAN class="p252 ft3">Cooperation with the Authorities of Member States</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr7 td13"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p136 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">Without prejudice to their privileges and immunities, it is the duty of all persons enjoying privileges and immunities under Articles 7, 8 and 9 to respect the laws and regulations of the Member State in whose territory they may operate in their official capacity.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p224 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">The SKAO shall cooperate at all times with the relevant authorities of Member States to facilitate the enforcement of their laws and to prevent the occurrence of any abuse in connection with the privileges and immunities referred to in this Protocol.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p195 ft3">Article 11</P>
<P class="p253 ft3">Purpose and waiver of Privileges and Immunities</P>
<P class="p136 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">The privileges and immunities provided for in this Protocol are not established for the personal benefit of those persons in whose favour they are accorded. Their purpose is solely to ensure unimpeded functioning of the SKAO and the complete independence of the persons to whom they are accorded.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p224 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft5">Competent authorities have a duty to waive any relevant immunity in all cases wherever retaining it would impede the course of justice and it can be waived without prejudicing the interests of the SKAO.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p222 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">The competent authorities referred to in the present Article, paragraph 2, are:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p254 ft3">a) Member States, in the case of their Representatives; b) The Council, in the case of the <NOBR>Director-General;</NOBR> and</P>
<P class="p224 ft3">c) The <NOBR>Director-General</NOBR> in the case of all Staff, Family members of Staff, Experts or any other person or persons enjoying immunities under this Protocol.</P>
<P class="p255 ft3">33</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_34">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p79 ft3">Prop. 2024/25:106 Bilaga 1</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p256 ft14">Annex B</P>
<P class="p257 ft3">Financial Protocol of the Square Kilometre Array Observatory</P>
<P class="p258 ft3">The Parties to the Convention,</P>
<P class="p259 ft3">AIMING to provide a policy framework under which all financial transactions and other such related financial matters will take place,</P>
<P class="p122 ft3">HAVE AGREED as follows:</P>
<P class="p165 ft3">Article 1</P>
<P class="p260 ft3">Definitions</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p171 ft3">For the purposes of this Protocol:</P>
<P class="p171 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">“Initial Funding Schedule” means the first Funding Schedule for the</SPAN></P>
<P class="p261 ft3">SKA Project;</P>
<P class="p167 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">“Financial Rules” means any rules, processes and procedures that implement the requirements of this Financial Protocol, and are approved by the Council from time to time.</SPAN></P>
